 facial rikgnishan ko anivaary karne se ab jin sevaaon ke liye aadhaar kii anivaaryta hai masalan banking, mobile oparator or sarkari yojanaon kaa laabh ke liye ab aadhaar othentication karaane ke liye facial rikgnishan karana hoga
 However, the Aadhaar data held by UIDAI does not yet contain the facial recognition data of any citizen
 UIDAI ke mutabik ab kevaisi karaate vakt photo dene ke saath-saath aadhaar othentication ke liye ab on-spot photo bhi khinchi jaaegi
 UIDAI has claimed that the facilitation of facial recognition will further improve the current authentication process
 philhal aadhaar othentication ke liye aankh kii putali (iris othentication) or ungali ke nishaan (fingerprint othentication) or mobile phone ke jariye otipiothentificationaki prakriya kii jaati he
 It is to be noted that this process is being done on the basis of a circular issued by the UIDAI on August 17, 2018
 UIDAI ke mutabik isse aadhaar kaarykram ko adhik samaveshi banaaya ja sakegaa
 This step will make Aadhaar authentication easier for those who face difficulty in Aadhaar verification through fingerprint
